\mbox{\Hypertarget{embroidermodder_8h_ab057e1afb884d1e29ecc02ebc883a8f1}\label{embroidermodder_8h_ab057e1afb884d1e29ecc02ebc883a8f1}} 
\index{embroidermodder.h@{embroidermodder.h}!Settings@{Settings}}
\index{Settings@{Settings}!embroidermodder.h@{embroidermodder.h}}
\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{Settings}{Settings}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef struct \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_settings__}{Settings\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{embroidermodder_8h_ab057e1afb884d1e29ecc02ebc883a8f1}{Settings}}}



Settings System. 

Rather than pollute the global namespace, we collect together all the global settings into a structure that stores them. This also allows us to create a complete copy of the settings for the purpose of restoring them if the user cancels out of the Settings Dialog.

Like all of our structs, it\textquotesingle{}s C99 compliant. \mbox{\Hypertarget{embroidermodder_8h_ac5795a0e93d9740c0f6a44ea312402bc}\label{embroidermodder_8h_ac5795a0e93d9740c0f6a44ea312402bc}} 
\index{embroidermodder.h@{embroidermodder.h}!UiObject@{UiObject}}
\index{UiObject@{UiObject}!embroidermodder.h@{embroidermodder.h}}
\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{UiObject}{UiObject}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef struct \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_ui_object__}{Ui\+Object\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{embroidermodder_8h_ac5795a0e93d9740c0f6a44ea312402bc}{Ui\+Object}}}



This covers the inbuilt designs\+: Dolphin, Snowflake and Heart. Covers Rotate, Scale and Point UI events. 

scale is how radii are stored if the object is a circle, or the semi-\/major and semi-\/minor axes if the object is an ellipse.

center perhaps should be the \char`\"{}anchor\char`\"{} instead which is the center for some objects and top left for rectangular objects.

Do angles need special storage? angle\+Ref, angle\+New

This chapter details how the source code achieves the design detailed in the previous chapter. For the low-\/level details, read the later chapters.

Dear Im\+Gui (CITATION NEEDED)\hypertarget{embroidermodder_8h_autotoc_md0}{}\doxyparagraph{Geometry Objects}\label{embroidermodder_8h_autotoc_md0}
At all times the Emb\+Pattern has all of the information about the pattern however, editing information like the rubber text labels needs to be stored during runtime. Also editing ghosts like when a rotate command is half executed.

To deal with this we have a generic object that can act as any other object that updates the associated pattern struct as changes as made.

Note that the editor state is seperate from this since that is per view, not per object.

Selecting is done via this interface. \mbox{\Hypertarget{embroidermodder_8h_a459ace9a6c614fe41b7f08ba91bc6dd4}\label{embroidermodder_8h_a459ace9a6c614fe41b7f08ba91bc6dd4}} 
\index{embroidermodder.h@{embroidermodder.h}!UndoHistory@{UndoHistory}}
\index{UndoHistory@{UndoHistory}!embroidermodder.h@{embroidermodder.h}}
\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{UndoHistory}{UndoHistory}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef struct \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_undo_history__}{Undo\+History\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{embroidermodder_8h_a459ace9a6c614fe41b7f08ba91bc6dd4}{Undo\+History}}}
